Local Open Scope cat.

Section BiadjunctionPreservation.
  Context {B₁ B₂ : bicat}
          {L : psfunctor B₁ B₂}
          (R : left_biadj_data L).

  Section PreserveProducts.
    Context (HB₁ : is_univalent_2_1 B₁)
            (HB₂ : is_univalent_2_1 B₂)
            {y₁ y₂ : B₂}
            (p : binprod_cone y₁ y₂)
            (Hp : has_binprod_ump p)
            (x : B₁).

    Definition right_biadj_preserves_binprod_1cell
      : bicat_of_univ_cats
          ⟦ univ_hom HB₁ x (psfunctor_binprod_cone R p)
            ,
            univalent_category_binproduct
              (univ_hom HB₁ x (R y₁))
              (univ_hom HB₁ x (R y₂)) ⟧
      := biadj_left_hom R x p
         ∙ postcomp_binprod_cone HB₂ p (L x)
         ∙ pair_functor (biadj_right_hom R x y₁) (biadj_right_hom R x y₂).

    
B₁, B₂: bicat
L: psfunctor B₁ B₂
R: left_biadj_data L
HB₁: is_univalent_2_1 B₁
HB₂: is_univalent_2_1 B₂
y₁, y₂: B₂
p: binprod_cone y₁ y₂
Hp: has_binprod_ump p
x: B₁
left_adjoint_equivalence
  right_biadj_preserves_binprod_1cell

    
B₁, B₂: bicat
L: psfunctor B₁ B₂

· right_biadj_preserves_binprod_nat_trans_data f₂ =

· # (pr1 right_biadj_preserves_binprod_1cell) α

B₁, B₂: bicat
L: psfunctor B₁ B₂
R: left_biadj_data L
HB₁: is_univalent_2_1 B₁
HB₂: is_univalent_2_1 B₂
y₁, y₂: B₂
p: binprod_cone y₁ y₂
Hp: has_binprod_ump p
x: B₁
f₁, f₂: univ_hom HB₁ x (psfunctor_binprod_cone R p)
α: univ_hom HB₁ x (psfunctor_binprod_cone R p) ⟦ f₁,
f₂ ⟧
(α ▹ binprod_cone_pr1 (psfunctor_binprod_cone R p))
· ((((((((f₂
          ◃ ((linvunitor (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
              • (((...) • (...))
                 ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))
             • rassociator (biadj_unit R (R p))
                 (# R (biadj_counit R p))
                 (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))))
         • lassociator f₂ (biadj_unit R (R p))
             (# R (biadj_counit R p)
              · # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))
        • lassociator (f₂ · biadj_unit R (R p))
            (# R (biadj_counit R p))
            (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))
       • (((psnaturality_of (biadj_unit R) f₂) ^-1
           ▹ # R (biadj_counit R p))
          ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))
      • (rassociator (biadj_unit R x) (# R (# L f₂))
           (# R (biadj_counit R p))
         ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))
     • rassociator (biadj_unit R x)
         (# R (# L f₂) · # R (biadj_counit R p))
         (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))
    • (biadj_unit R x
       ◃ (psfunctor_comp R (# L f₂) (biadj_counit R p)
          ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))))
   • (biadj_unit R x
      ◃ psfunctor_comp R (# L f₂ · biadj_counit R p)
          (binprod_cone_pr1 p))) =
((((((((f₁
        ◃ ((linvunitor (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
            • (((...) • (...))
               ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))
           • rassociator (biadj_unit R (R p))
               (# R (biadj_counit R p))
               (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))))
       • lassociator f₁ (biadj_unit R (R p))
           (# R (biadj_counit R p)
            · # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))
      • lassociator (f₁ · biadj_unit R (R p))
          (# R (biadj_counit R p))
          (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))
     • (((psnaturality_of (biadj_unit R) f₁) ^-1
         ▹ # R (biadj_counit R p))
        ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))
    • (rassociator (biadj_unit R x) (# R (# L f₁))
         (# R (biadj_counit R p))
       ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))
   • rassociator (biadj_unit R x)
       (# R (# L f₁) · # R (biadj_counit R p))
       (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))
  • (biadj_unit R x
     ◃ (psfunctor_comp R (# L f₁) (biadj_counit R p)
        ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))))
 • (biadj_unit R x
    ◃ psfunctor_comp R (# L f₁ · biadj_counit R p)
        (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))
· (biadj_unit R x
   ◃ ## R
       ((## L α ▹ biadj_counit R p)
        ▹ binprod_cone_pr1 p))

        
B₁, B₂: bicat
L: psfunctor B₁ B₂
R: left_biadj_data L
HB₁: is_univalent_2_1 B₁
HB₂: is_univalent_2_1 B₂
y₁, y₂: B₂
p: binprod_cone y₁ y₂
Hp: has_binprod_ump p

(f₁
 ◃ (linvunitor (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
    • ((((biadj_triangle_r R) ^-1 p
         • (lunitor
              (((λ X : B₂,
                 biadj_unit (pr1 R) (pr1 R X))
                · ((λ X : B₂, id₁ (pr1 R (...)))
                   · ((λ X : B₂, # (...) (...))
                      · (λ X : B₂, id₁ (...))))) p)
            • (biadj_unit (pr1 R) (pr1 R p)
               ◃ (lunitor
                    (# (pr1 R)
                       (biadj_counit (pr1 R) p)
                     · id₁ (pr1 R p))
                  • runitor
                      (# (pr1 R)
                         (biadj_counit (pr1 R) p))))))
        ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
       • rassociator (biadj_unit R (R p))
           (# R (biadj_counit R p))
           (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))))
• ((α
    ▹ biadj_unit R (R p)
      · (# R (biadj_counit R p)
         · # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))
   • (lassociator f₂ (biadj_unit R (R p))
        (# R (biadj_counit R p)
         · # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
      • (lassociator (f₂ · biadj_unit R (R p))
           (# R (biadj_counit R p))
           (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
         • ((((psnaturality_of (biadj_unit R) f₂) ^-1
              ▹ # R (biadj_counit R p))
             ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
            • ((rassociator (biadj_unit R x)
                  (# R (# L f₂))
                  (# R (biadj_counit R p))
                ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))

                     · # R (biadj_counit R p))
                    (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))

                      ◃ (psfunctor_comp R (# L f₂)
                           (biadj_counit R p)
                         ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))
                     • (biadj_unit R x
                        ◃ psfunctor_comp R
                            (# L f₂ · biadj_counit R p)
                            (binprod_cone_pr1 p))))))))) =
(f₁
 ◃ (linvunitor (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
    • ((((biadj_triangle_r R) ^-1 p
         • (lunitor
              (((λ X : B₂,
                 biadj_unit (pr1 R) (pr1 R X))
                · ((λ X : B₂, id₁ (pr1 R (...)))
                   · ((λ X : B₂, # (...) (...))
                      · (λ X : B₂, id₁ (...))))) p)
            • (biadj_unit (pr1 R) (pr1 R p)
               ◃ (lunitor
                    (# (pr1 R)
                       (biadj_counit (pr1 R) p)
                     · id₁ (pr1 R p))
                  • runitor
                      (# (pr1 R)
                         (biadj_counit (pr1 R) p))))))
        ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
       • rassociator (biadj_unit R (R p))
           (# R (biadj_counit R p))
           (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))))
• (lassociator f₁ (biadj_unit R (R p))
     (# R (biadj_counit R p)
      · # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
   • (lassociator (f₁ · biadj_unit R (R p))

        (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))

                              ▹ biadj_counit R p)

                        (biadj_counit R p)
                      ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))
                  • (biadj_unit R x
                     ◃ psfunctor_comp R
                         (# L f₂ · biadj_counit R p)
                         (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))))))) =
lassociator f₁ (biadj_unit R (R p))
  (# R (biadj_counit R p) · # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
• (lassociator (f₁ · biadj_unit R (R p))
     (# R (biadj_counit R p))
     (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
   • ((((psnaturality_of (biadj_unit R) f₁) ^-1
        ▹ # R (biadj_counit R p))
       ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
      • ((rassociator (biadj_unit R x) (# R (# L f₁))
            (# R (biadj_counit R p))
          ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
         • (rassociator (biadj_unit R x)
              (# R (# L f₁) · # R (biadj_counit R p))
              (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
            • ((biadj_unit R x
                ◃ (psfunctor_comp R (# L f₁)
                     (biadj_counit R p)
                   ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))
               • ((biadj_unit R x
                   ◃ psfunctor_comp R
                       (# L f₁ · biadj_counit R p)
                       (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
                  • (biadj_unit R x
                     ◃ ## R
                         ((## L α ▹ biadj_counit R p)
                          ▹ binprod_cone_pr1 p))))))))

             ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))
         • ((biadj_unit R x
             ◃ psfunctor_comp R
                 (# L f₁ · biadj_counit R p)
                 (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
            • (biadj_unit R x
               ◃ ## R
                   ((## L α ▹ biadj_counit R p)
                    ▹ binprod_cone_pr1 p))))))

f₂ ⟧
(((psnaturality_of (biadj_unit R) f₁) ^-1
  ▹ # R (biadj_counit R p)) ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
• ((rassociator (biadj_unit R x) (# R (# L f₁))
      (# R (biadj_counit R p))
    ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
   • (((biadj_unit R x
        ◃ psfunctor_comp R (# L f₁) (biadj_counit R p))
       ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
      • (rassociator (biadj_unit R x)
           (# R (# L f₁ · biadj_counit R p))
           (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
         • ((biadj_unit R x
             ◃ psfunctor_comp R
                 (# L f₁ · biadj_counit R p)
                 (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
            • (biadj_unit R x
               ◃ ## R
                   ((## L α ▹ biadj_counit R p)
                    ▹ binprod_cone_pr1 p)))))) =
(((α ▹ biadj_unit R (R p)) ▹ # R (biadj_counit R p))
 ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
• ((((psnaturality_of (biadj_unit R) f₂) ^-1
     ▹ # R (biadj_counit R p))
    ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
   • ((rassociator (biadj_unit R x) (# R (# L f₂))
         (# R (biadj_counit R p))
       ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))

           ◃ psfunctor_comp R (# L f₂)
               (biadj_counit R p))

α: univ_hom HB₁ x (psfunctor_binprod_cone R p) ⟦ f₁,
f₂ ⟧
(((psnaturality_of (biadj_unit R) f₁) ^-1
  ▹ # R (biadj_counit R p)) ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
• ((((biadj_unit R x ◃ ## R (## L α))
     ▹ # R (biadj_counit R p))
    ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
   • ((rassociator (biadj_unit R x) (# R (# L f₂))
         (# R (biadj_counit R p))
       ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
      • (((biadj_unit R x
           ◃ psfunctor_comp R (# L f₂)
               (biadj_counit R p))
          ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
         • (rassociator (biadj_unit R x)
              (# R (# L f₂ · biadj_counit R p))
              (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
            • (biadj_unit R x
               ◃ psfunctor_comp R
                   (# L f₂ · biadj_counit R p)
                   (binprod_cone_pr1 p)))))) = ?b

  ◃ psfunctor_comp R (# L f₂) (biadj_counit R p))
 ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
• (rassociator (biadj_unit R x)
     (# R (# L f₂ · biadj_counit R p))
     (# R (binprod_cone_pr1 p))
   • (biadj_unit R x
      ◃ psfunctor_comp R (# L f₂ · biadj_counit R p)
          (binprod_cone_pr1 p))) = ?t2

  ▹ # R (biadj_counit R p)) ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr2 p))

      (# R (biadj_counit R p))
    ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr2 p))

               (biadj_counit R p)

         • ((biadj_unit R x

                 (binprod_cone_pr2 p))
            • (biadj_unit R x
               ◃ ## R
                   ((## L α ▹ biadj_counit R p)
                    ▹ binprod_cone_pr2 p)))))) = ?b

   ◃ psfunctor_comp R (# L f₂) (biadj_counit R p)) =

        ◃ psfunctor_comp R (# L f₂) (biadj_counit R p))
       ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr2 p))
      • (rassociator (biadj_unit R x)
           (# R (# L f₂ · biadj_counit R p))
           (# R (binprod_cone_pr2 p))
         • (biadj_unit R x
            ◃ psfunctor_comp R
                (# L f₂ · biadj_counit R p)
                (binprod_cone_pr2 p))))) =
(rassociator (biadj_unit R x) (# R (# L f₁))
   (# R (biadj_counit R p)) ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr2 p))
• (((biadj_unit R x
     ◃ psfunctor_comp R (# L f₁) (biadj_counit R p))
    ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr2 p))
   • (rassociator (biadj_unit R x)
        (# R (# L f₁ · biadj_counit R p))
        (# R (binprod_cone_pr2 p))
      • ((biadj_unit R x
          ◃ psfunctor_comp R
              (# L f₁ · biadj_counit R p)
              (binprod_cone_pr2 p))
         • (biadj_unit R x
            ◃ ## R
                ((## L α ▹ biadj_counit R p)
                 ▹ binprod_cone_pr2 p)))))

B₁, B₂: bicat
L: psfunctor B₁ B₂
R: left_biadj_data L
HB₁: is_univalent_2_1 B₁
HB₂: is_univalent_2_1 B₂
y₁, y₂: B₂
p: binprod_cone y₁ y₂
Hp: has_binprod_ump p
x: B₁
c: univ_hom HB₁ x (psfunctor_binprod_cone R p)
is_invertible_2cell
  ((((((((# (Identity.id_psfunctor B₁) c
          ◃ ((linvunitor (# R (binprod_cone_pr2 p))
              • (((... • ...) • (... ◃ ...))
                 ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr2 p)))
             • rassociator (biadj_unit R (R p))
                 (# R (biadj_counit R p))
                 (# R (binprod_cone_pr2 p))))
         • lassociator
             (# (Identity.id_psfunctor B₁) c)
             (biadj_unit R (R p))
             (# R (biadj_counit R p)
              · # R (binprod_cone_pr2 p)))
        • lassociator
            (# (Identity.id_psfunctor B₁) c
             · biadj_unit R (R p))
            (# R (biadj_counit R p))
            (# R (binprod_cone_pr2 p)))
       • (((psnaturality_of (biadj_unit R) c) ^-1
           ▹ # R (biadj_counit R p))
          ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr2 p)))
      • (rassociator (biadj_unit R x)
           (# (Composition.comp_psfunctor R L) c)
           (# R (biadj_counit R p))
         ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr2 p)))
     • rassociator (biadj_unit R x)
         (# (Composition.comp_psfunctor R L) c
          · # R (biadj_counit R p))
         (# R (binprod_cone_pr2 p)))
    • (biadj_unit R x
       ◃ (psfunctor_comp R (# L c) (biadj_counit R p)
          ▹ # R (binprod_cone_pr2 p))))
   • (biadj_unit R x
      ◃ psfunctor_comp R (# L c · biadj_counit R p)
          (binprod_cone_pr2 p)))

        is_iso ; apply property_from_invertible_2cell.
    Defined.

     (psfunctor_binprod_cone R p) x)
  right_biadj_preserves_binprod_1cell

  End PreserveProducts.
